                <div class="txtNew" data-min-height="496" data-packed="false" id="comp-jhw441dl" style="top:660px;bottom:;left:326px;right:;width:433px;height:auto;position:absolute;min-height:496px;margin-left:calc((100% - 980px) * 0.5)">
                 <p class="font_8">
                  For the first time in its' 94-year history, the Rotary Club of Letchworth Garden City has a woman among its ranks. Retired Letchworth teacher Yvonne Sonnen is our first woman member since the club started in 1924.
                 </p>
                 <p class="font_8">
                 </p>
                 <p class="font_8">
                  Rotary abandoned its men-only rule in 1989 since when more than 250,000 women worldwide have become members. And Yvonne, a former Year 6 teacher at Wilbury Primary School, is delighted to be now leading the way at the Rotary Club of Letchworth Garden City.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  " I feel very honoured to have been accepted as the club's latest recruit. I have always admired the community ethos of Rotary and particularly the links it has to education and helping young people in the area wherever it can" she says.
                  <br/>
                  <br/>
                  "There's a role for both men and women in the organisation. I don't expect I'll be the club's only female member for very long.
                 </p>
                 <p class="font_8">
                  I know a number of women keen to join.
                  <br/>
                 </p>
                 <p class="font_8">
                  " I'm delighted we've made club history " said Club President Peter Jackson " We've been open to ladies as well as gentlemen for almost 30 years. But I think quite a few women didn't fancy actually being the first one to join us! Now, thanks to Yvonne, that's changed forever. "
                  <br/>
                 </p>
                 <p class="font_8">
                  Yvonne, who lives on Fairfield Park, joins husband Bryan - a club member for more than 10 years and a former Club President.
                 </p>
                 <p class="font_8">
                  <span class="wixGuard">
                   
                  </span>
                 </p>
